* Rsync to hpcc

```bash
rsync -avP \
    ~/data/dna-seq/xjy/clean_data/ \
    wangq@202.119.37.251:data/dna-seq/xjy/clean_data

rsync -avP \
    ~/data/dna-seq/xjy/raw_data/ \
    wangq@202.119.37.251:data/dna-seq/xjy/raw_data

# rsync -avP wangq@202.119.37.251:data/dna-seq/xjy/ ~/data/dna-seq/xjy

```

# m07, 蜡梅


## m07: download

```bash
mkdir -p ~/data/dna-seq/xjy/m07/2_illumina
cd ~/data/dna-seq/xjy/m07/2_illumina

ln -s ~/data/dna-seq/xjy/clean_data/m07_H3J5KDMXX_L1_1.clean.fq.gz R1.fq.gz
ln -s ~/data/dna-seq/xjy/clean_data/m07_H3J5KDMXX_L1_2.clean.fq.gz R2.fq.gz

```

## m07: template

Restrict cov2 to 240x of 1M size because of contaminations of *Pseudomonas*

```bash
WORKING_DIR=${HOME}/data/dna-seq/xjy
BASE_NAME=m07

cd ${WORKING_DIR}/${BASE_NAME}

rm -f *.sh
anchr template \
    . \
    --basename ${BASE_NAME} \
    --queue mpi \
    --genome 1000000 \
    --fastqc \
    --kmergenie \
    --insertsize \
    --sgapreqc \
    --sgastats \
    --trim2 "--dedupe --tile --cutoff 30 --cutk 31" \
    --qual2 "25" \
    --len2 "60" \
    --filter "adapter,phix,artifact" \
    --mergereads \
    --ecphase "1,2,3" \
    --cov2 "40 80 120 160 240" \
    --tadpole \
    --splitp 100 \
    --statp 2 \
    --fillanchor \
    --redoanchors \
    --parallel 24

```

## m07: run

```bash
WORKING_DIR=${HOME}/data/dna-seq/xjy
BASE_NAME=m07

cd ${WORKING_DIR}/${BASE_NAME}
#rm -fr 4_*/ 6_*/ 7_*/ 8_*/ && rm -fr 2_illumina/trim 2_illumina/mergereads statReads.md 

bash 0_bsub.sh
#bkill -J "${BASE_NAME}-*"

#bash 0_master.sh
#bash 0_cleanup.sh

```

# m08, 祡楠


## m08: download

```bash
mkdir -p ~/data/dna-seq/xjy/m08/2_illumina
cd ~/data/dna-seq/xjy/m08/2_illumina

ln -s ~/data/dna-seq/xjy/clean_data/m08_H3J5KDMXX_L1_1.clean.fq.gz R1.fq.gz
ln -s ~/data/dna-seq/xjy/clean_data/m08_H3J5KDMXX_L1_2.clean.fq.gz R2.fq.gz

```

## m08: template

`--queue largemem` because of `ecphase 2: OutOfMemoryError`

```bash
WORKING_DIR=${HOME}/data/dna-seq/xjy
BASE_NAME=m08

cd ${WORKING_DIR}/${BASE_NAME}

rm -f *.sh
anchr template \
    . \
    --basename ${BASE_NAME} \
    --queue largemem \
    --genome 1000000 \
    --fastqc \
    --kmergenie \
    --insertsize \
    --sgapreqc \
    --sgastats \
    --trim2 "--dedupe --tile --cutoff 30 --cutk 31" \
    --qual2 "25" \
    --len2 "60" \
    --filter "adapter,phix,artifact" \
    --mergereads \
    --ecphase "1,2,3" \
    --cov2 "40 80 120 160 240 320" \
    --tadpole \
    --splitp 100 \
    --statp 2 \
    --fillanchor \
    --parallel 24

```

## m08: run

```bash
WORKING_DIR=${HOME}/data/dna-seq/xjy
BASE_NAME=m08

cd ${WORKING_DIR}/${BASE_NAME}
#rm -fr 4_*/ 6_*/ 7_*/ 8_*/ 2_illumina/trim 2_illumina/mergereads statReads.md 

bash 0_bsub.sh
#bash 0_master.sh

#bash 0_cleanup.sh

```

# m15, 铁线莲


## m15: download

```bash
mkdir -p ~/data/dna-seq/xjy/m15/2_illumina
cd ~/data/dna-seq/xjy/m15/2_illumina

ln -s ~/data/dna-seq/xjy/clean_data/m15_H3HTCDMXX_L1_1.clean.fq.gz R1.fq.gz
ln -s ~/data/dna-seq/xjy/clean_data/m15_H3HTCDMXX_L1_2.clean.fq.gz R2.fq.gz
```


## m15: template

```bash
WORKING_DIR=${HOME}/data/dna-seq/xjy
BASE_NAME=m15

cd ${WORKING_DIR}/${BASE_NAME}

rm -f *.sh
anchr template \
    . \
    --basename ${BASE_NAME} \
    --queue mpi \
    --genome 1000000 \
    --fastqc \
    --kmergenie \
    --insertsize \
    --sgapreqc \
    --sgastats \
    --trim2 "--dedupe --tile --cutoff 30 --cutk 31" \
    --qual2 "25" \
    --len2 "60" \
    --filter "adapter,phix,artifact" \
    --mergereads \
    --ecphase "1,2,3" \
    --cov2 "40 80 120 160 240 320" \
    --tadpole \
    --splitp 100 \
    --statp 2 \
    --fillanchor \
    --parallel 24

```

## m15: run

```bash
WORKING_DIR=${HOME}/data/dna-seq/xjy
BASE_NAME=m15

cd ${WORKING_DIR}/${BASE_NAME}
#rm -fr 4_*/ 6_*/ 7_*/ 8_*/ 2_illumina/trim 2_illumina/mergereads statReads.md 

bash 0_bsub.sh
#bash 0_master.sh

#bash 0_cleanup.sh

```

# m17, 樟


## m17: download

```bash
mkdir -p ~/data/dna-seq/xjy/m17/2_illumina
cd ~/data/dna-seq/xjy/m17/2_illumina

ln -s ~/data/dna-seq/xjy/clean_data/m17_H3J5KDMXX_L1_1.clean.fq.gz R1.fq.gz
ln -s ~/data/dna-seq/xjy/clean_data/m17_H3J5KDMXX_L1_2.clean.fq.gz R2.fq.gz

```


## m17: template

```bash
WORKING_DIR=${HOME}/data/dna-seq/xjy
BASE_NAME=m17

cd ${WORKING_DIR}/${BASE_NAME}

rm -f *.sh
anchr template \
    . \
    --basename ${BASE_NAME} \
    --queue mpi \
    --genome 1000000 \
    --fastqc \
    --kmergenie \
    --insertsize \
    --sgapreqc \
    --sgastats \
    --trim2 "--dedupe --tile --cutoff 30 --cutk 31" \
    --qual2 "25" \
    --len2 "60" \
    --filter "adapter,phix,artifact" \
    --mergereads \
    --ecphase "1,2,3" \
    --cov2 "40 80 120 160 240 320" \
    --tadpole \
    --splitp 100 \
    --statp 2 \
    --fillanchor \
    --parallel 24

```

## m17: run

```bash
WORKING_DIR=${HOME}/data/dna-seq/xjy
BASE_NAME=m17

cd ${WORKING_DIR}/${BASE_NAME}
#rm -fr 4_*/ 6_*/ 7_*/ 8_*/ 2_illumina/trim 2_illumina/mergereads statReads.md 

bash 0_bsub.sh
#bash 0_master.sh

#bash 0_cleanup.sh

```

# m19, 青城细辛


## m19: download

```bash
mkdir -p ~/data/dna-seq/xjy/m19/2_illumina
cd ~/data/dna-seq/xjy/m19/2_illumina

ln -s ~/data/dna-seq/xjy/clean_data/m19_H3J5KDMXX_L1_1.clean.fq.gz R1.fq.gz
ln -s ~/data/dna-seq/xjy/clean_data/m19_H3J5KDMXX_L1_2.clean.fq.gz R2.fq.gz

```


## m19: template

```bash
WORKING_DIR=${HOME}/data/dna-seq/xjy
BASE_NAME=m19

cd ${WORKING_DIR}/${BASE_NAME}

rm -f *.sh
anchr template \
    . \
    --basename ${BASE_NAME} \
    --queue mpi \
    --genome 1000000 \
    --fastqc \
    --kmergenie \
    --insertsize \
    --sgapreqc \
    --sgastats \
    --trim2 "--dedupe --tile --cutoff 30 --cutk 31" \
    --qual2 "25" \
    --len2 "60" \
    --filter "adapter,phix,artifact" \
    --mergereads \
    --ecphase "1,2,3" \
    --cov2 "40 80 120 160 240 320" \
    --tadpole \
    --splitp 100 \
    --statp 2 \
    --fillanchor \
    --parallel 24

```

## m19: run

```bash
WORKING_DIR=${HOME}/data/dna-seq/xjy
BASE_NAME=m19

cd ${WORKING_DIR}/${BASE_NAME}
#rm -fr 4_*/ 6_*/ 7_*/ 8_*/ 2_illumina/trim 2_illumina/mergereads statReads.md 

bash 0_bsub.sh
#bash 0_master.sh

#bash 0_cleanup.sh

```

# m20, 石刁柏


## m20: download

```bash
mkdir -p ~/data/dna-seq/xjy/m20/2_illumina
cd ~/data/dna-seq/xjy/m20/2_illumina

ln -s ~/data/dna-seq/xjy/clean_data/m20_H3J5KDMXX_L1_1.clean.fq.gz R1.fq.gz
ln -s ~/data/dna-seq/xjy/clean_data/m20_H3J5KDMXX_L1_2.clean.fq.gz R2.fq.gz
```


## m20: template

细胞器 DNA 比例较大, 不需要 320x.

最后的 contigs 很可能有问题.

```bash
WORKING_DIR=${HOME}/data/dna-seq/xjy
BASE_NAME=m20

cd ${WORKING_DIR}/${BASE_NAME}

rm -f *.sh
anchr template \
    . \
    --basename ${BASE_NAME} \
    --queue mpi \
    --genome 1000000 \
    --fastqc \
    --kmergenie \
    --insertsize \
    --sgapreqc \
    --sgastats \
    --trim2 "--dedupe --tile --cutoff 30 --cutk 31" \
    --sample2 1000 \
    --qual2 "25" \
    --len2 "60" \
    --filter "adapter,phix,artifact" \
    --mergereads \
    --ecphase "1,2,3" \
    --cov2 "40 80 120 160 240" \
    --tadpole \
    --splitp 100 \
    --statp 2 \
    --fillanchor \
    --redoanchors \
    --parallel 24

```

## m20: run

```bash
WORKING_DIR=${HOME}/data/dna-seq/xjy
BASE_NAME=m20

cd ${WORKING_DIR}/${BASE_NAME}
#rm -fr 4_*/ 6_*/ 7_*/ 8_*/ 2_illumina/trim 2_illumina/mergereads statReads.md 

bash 0_bsub.sh
#bash 0_master.sh

#bash 0_cleanup.sh

```

# m22, 多穗金粟兰

## m22: download

```bash
mkdir -p ~/data/dna-seq/xjy/m22/2_illumina
cd ~/data/dna-seq/xjy/m22/2_illumina

ln -fs ~/data/dna-seq/xjy/clean_data/m22_H3JJGDMXX_L1_1.clean.fq.gz R1.fq.gz
ln -fs ~/data/dna-seq/xjy/clean_data/m22_H3JJGDMXX_L1_2.clean.fq.gz R2.fq.gz

```

## m22: template

* Contaminated by *Sphingobium*

* `-Xmx` is not correctly set by largemem
    * `--insertsize` and `--mergereads` failed in hpcc
    * `KmerCountExact`: OutOfMemoryError

* `--cutoff 200`: `| 7_mergeAnchors.anchors | 2057 | 122329 | 61 |`

```bash
WORKING_DIR=${HOME}/data/dna-seq/xjy
BASE_NAME=m22

cd ${WORKING_DIR}/${BASE_NAME}

rm -f *.sh
anchr template \
    . \
    --basename ${BASE_NAME} \
    --queue mpi \
    --genome 1000000 \
    --fastqc \
    --kmergenie \
    --insertsize \
    --sgapreqc \
    --sgastats \
    --trim2 "--dedupe --tile --cutoff 30 --cutk 31" \
    --qual2 "25" \
    --len2 "60" \
    --filter "adapter,phix,artifact" \
    --mergereads \
    --ecphase "1,2,3" \
    --cov2 "40 80 120 160 240" \
    --tadpole \
    --splitp 100 \
    --statp 2 \
    --fillanchor \
    --parallel 24

```

## m22: run

```bash
WORKING_DIR=${HOME}/data/dna-seq/xjy
BASE_NAME=m22

cd ${WORKING_DIR}/${BASE_NAME}
#rm -fr 4_*/ 6_*/ 7_*/ 8_*/ && rm -fr 2_illumina/trim 2_illumina/mergereads statReads.md 

bash 0_bsub.sh
#bash 0_master.sh

#bash 0_cleanup.sh

```

# mt203, 五娅果


## mt203: download

```bash
mkdir -p ~/data/dna-seq/xjy/mt203/2_illumina
cd ~/data/dna-seq/xjy/mt203/2_illumina

ln -s ../../raw_data/MT203_H3LCYDMXX_L1_1.fq.gz R1.fq.gz
ln -s ../../raw_data/MT203_H3LCYDMXX_L1_2.fq.gz R2.fq.gz

```


## mt203: template

```bash
WORKING_DIR=${HOME}/data/dna-seq/xjy
BASE_NAME=mt203

cd ${WORKING_DIR}/${BASE_NAME}

rm -f *.sh
anchr template \
    . \
    --basename ${BASE_NAME} \
    --queue mpi \
    --genome 1000000 \
    --fastqc \
    --kmergenie \
    --insertsize \
    --sgapreqc \
    --sgastats \
    --trim2 "--dedupe --tile --cutoff 20 --cutk 31" \
    --qual2 "25" \
    --len2 "60" \
    --filter "adapter,phix,artifact" \
    --mergereads \
    --ecphase "1,2,3" \
    --cov2 "40 80 120 160 240 320" \
    --tadpole \
    --splitp 100 \
    --statp 2 \
    --fillanchor \
    --parallel 24

```

## mt203: run

```bash
WORKING_DIR=${HOME}/data/dna-seq/xjy
BASE_NAME=mt203

cd ${WORKING_DIR}/${BASE_NAME}
#rm -fr 4_*/ 6_*/ 7_*/ 8_*/ 2_illumina/trim 2_illumina/mergereads statReads.md 

bash 0_bsub.sh
#bash 0_master.sh

#bash 0_cleanup.sh

```

# mt301, 金鱼藻


## mt301: download

```bash
mkdir -p ~/data/dna-seq/xjy/mt301/2_illumina
cd ~/data/dna-seq/xjy/mt301/2_illumina

ln -s ../../raw_data/mt301_H73Y3DMXX_L1_1.fq.gz R1.fq.gz
ln -s ../../raw_data/mt301_H73Y3DMXX_L1_2.fq.gz R2.fq.gz

```

## mt301: template

```bash
WORKING_DIR=${HOME}/data/dna-seq/xjy
BASE_NAME=mt301

cd ${WORKING_DIR}/${BASE_NAME}

rm -f *.sh
anchr template \
    . \
    --basename ${BASE_NAME} \
    --queue mpi \
    --genome 1000000 \
    --fastqc \
    --kmergenie \
    --insertsize \
    --sgapreqc \
    --sgastats \
    --trim2 "--dedupe --tile --cutoff 20 --cutk 31" \
    --qual2 "25" \
    --len2 "60" \
    --filter "adapter,phix,artifact" \
    --mergereads \
    --ecphase "1,2,3" \
    --cov2 "40 80 120 160 240 320" \
    --tadpole \
    --splitp 100 \
    --statp 2 \
    --fillanchor \
    --parallel 24

```

## mt301: run

```bash
WORKING_DIR=${HOME}/data/dna-seq/xjy
BASE_NAME=mt301

cd ${WORKING_DIR}/${BASE_NAME}
#rm -fr 4_*/ 6_*/ 7_*/ 8_*/ 2_illumina/trim 2_illumina/mergereads statReads.md 

bash 0_bsub.sh
#bash 0_master.sh

#bash 0_cleanup.sh

```

## mt302: download

```bash
mkdir -p ~/data/dna-seq/xjy/mt302/2_illumina
```

## mt302: template

```bash
WORKING_DIR=${HOME}/data/dna-seq/xjy

cd ${WORKING_DIR}/${BASE_NAME}

anchr template \
    . \
    --basename ${BASE_NAME} \

    --fastqc \

    --insertsize \
    --sgapreqc \
    --sgastats \
```

# mt401, 草珊瑚

简化法分离线粒体DNA测序, 会有核污染, 需要看下线粒体 DNA 所占比例, 为今后的3代测序提供参考.

## mt401: download

```bash
mkdir -p ~/data/dna-seq/xjy/mt401/2_illumina
cd ~/data/dna-seq/xjy/mt401/2_illumina

ln -s ../../raw_data/mt401_PE400_R1.fq.gz R1.fq.gz
ln -s ../../raw_data/mt401_PE400_R2.fq.gz R2.fq.gz

```

## mt401: template

```bash
WORKING_DIR=${HOME}/data/dna-seq/xjy
BASE_NAME=mt401

cd ${WORKING_DIR}/${BASE_NAME}

rm -f *.sh
anchr template \
    . \
    --basename ${BASE_NAME} \
    --queue mpi \
    --genome 1000000 \
    --fastqc \
    --kmergenie \
    --insertsize \
    --sgapreqc \
    --sgastats \
    --trim2 "--dedupe --tile --cutoff 20 --cutk 31" \
    --qual2 "25" \
    --len2 "60" \
    --filter "adapter,phix,artifact" \
    --mergereads \
    --ecphase "1,2,3" \
    --cov2 "40 80 120 160 240 320" \
    --tadpole \
    --splitp 100 \
    --statp 2 \
    --fillanchor \
    --parallel 24

```

## mt401: run

```bash
WORKING_DIR=${HOME}/data/dna-seq/xjy
BASE_NAME=mt401

cd ${WORKING_DIR}/${BASE_NAME}
#rm -fr 4_*/ 6_*/ 7_*/ 8_*/ 2_illumina/trim 2_illumina/mergereads statReads.md 

bash 0_bsub.sh
#bash 0_master.sh

#bash 0_cleanup.sh

```

# mt402, 十数樟

未分离线粒体DNA, 总DNA直接测序.

## mt402: download

```bash
mkdir -p ~/data/dna-seq/xjy/mt402/2_illumina
cd ~/data/dna-seq/xjy/mt402/2_illumina

ln -s ../../raw_data/mt402_PE400_R1.fq.gz R1.fq.gz
ln -s ../../raw_data/mt402_PE400_R2.fq.gz R2.fq.gz

```

## mt402: template

```bash
WORKING_DIR=${HOME}/data/dna-seq/xjy
BASE_NAME=mt402

cd ${WORKING_DIR}/${BASE_NAME}

rm -f *.sh
anchr template \
    . \
    --basename ${BASE_NAME} \
    --queue mpi \
    --genome 1000000 \
    --fastqc \
    --kmergenie \
    --insertsize \
    --sgapreqc \
    --sgastats \
    --trim2 "--dedupe --tile --cutoff 20 --cutk 31" \
    --qual2 "25" \
    --len2 "60" \
    --filter "adapter,phix,artifact" \
    --mergereads \
    --ecphase "1,2,3" \
    --cov2 "40 80 120 160 240 320" \
    --tadpole \
    --splitp 100 \
    --statp 2 \
    --fillanchor \
    --parallel 24

```

## mt402: run

```bash

bash 0_bsub.sh
#bash 0_master.sh

#bash 0_cleanup.sh

```

# Create tarballs

* Illumina QC
    * FastQC
    * InsertSize
* Other assemblies
    * Spades
    * Megahit
    * Platanus
* Our assemblies
* Unreliable parts of our assemblies
* Short gaps (fill gaps shorter than 2000 bp)

```bash
cd ${HOME}/data/dna-seq/xjy

for BASE_NAME in m07 m08 m15 m17 m19 m20 m22 mt203 mt301 mt302 mt401 mt402; do
    echo >&2 "==> ${BASE_NAME}"
    pushd ${HOME}/data/dna-seq/xjy/${BASE_NAME}

    if [ -e ../${BASE_NAME}.tar.gz ]; then
        echo >&2 "    ${BASE_NAME}.tar.gz exists"
    else
        tar -czvf \
            ../${BASE_NAME}.tar.gz \
            2_illumina/fastqc/*.html \
            2_illumina/insertSize/*.pdf \
            2_illumina/sgaPreQC/*.pdf \
            7_mergeAnchors/anchor.merge.fasta \
            7_mergeAnchors/others.non-contained.fasta \
            7_anchorLong/contig.fasta \
            7_anchorFill/contig.fasta
    fi

    popd > /dev/null
done

```
